Lungkhamna thu kigen nawnlou in;
Kikhen lungkhamna thuak a maute,
Nopna kha jak in lengkhawm ding uh.

359 A Vak Ah Ka Leng Ding

    Tangtawn in a vak ah ka leng ding.

360 Mual Khumta Uh

Vankhama

363 Pathian In Hon Ching Hen

365 Van Khawpi Pul

Rev. Thangngur

366 A Sung Ah Hong Teng In

Saptawna

Zion Temple kullou Inn lam nawnta ung,
Nang koute Siampi Lian Na hi;

367 Khuavannuai Vaihawm Ding

Ngai in Amah hong paikik ding hi,
Thupina tawh van mei tung ah;
I Mang uh Immanuel in,
Khuavannuai vaihawm ding.

    Mi kim, nam kim, A Mangtutphah mai ah,
    Kikhawm ding a kipuang ding hi;
    Salem Kumpipa mai ah aw,
    Bang ka gen sam ding hiam?

A mel thupi nibang a tang ah,
Dawite leh melma khempeuhte;
Tatsate i lungdam ni in,
Lau in lingta ding uh.

Lei lungkham buaina lambang kheng in,
Pai masa leh angel siang tawh;
Salem thak tual nuam a leng in,
Hin tawp omlou ding hi.

Lungkham leh naubang kah omlou ding,

368 Khua Vakta Ding

Mang bang in phatna zaila in awi uh,
Mizatam singta kuamah simsenglouh,
Hong hita ding.

    Van khawsimpi ah vanmi a sim ua,

372 Aw Kalvari, Aw Kalvari

384 Zekailou In Seem In

Ngaidih, manthatna janmial mulkimhuai nuai ah,
Laukha simsenglouh mang ding om uh;
Suahtakna thu theilou a mangjel te,
Nang na kitheihmawhbawl mai ding a hiam?
Amaute huh ding mi ngai uh,
Aw kinmeng in kinmeng in mang jel uh.

    Aw, zekai lou in sem in hun beima in,
    Tangtawn hinna lam theilou a mangte;
    Hinna Vak lam ah honpi inla,
    Tangtawn tangtawn a mangnawn lou ding in.

"Manthatna lampi jui a paite pi ding in,
Kei dia sem di'n kua a hiam kuan ding?
Sisan a ka leisa khial a mangte,
Aw amaute ka itna dai tuanlou;
Khelhna meipi'n sunchin tuam hi,
Tuin thou in, kuan in zong in, sem in."

Endih, tangtawn manthatna meipi kai nuai ah,
Mangthang panpih ngen aw te ngai in;
Tua aw gingte na ngilh mai ding hiam?
Amau huh di'n Pathian galvan la in;
Hanmial lam juan in kuankhia in,
Khial a puksate hon pikik meng in.

Tua tangthupha vakna lampi theisa eite'n,
Sihna janmial nuai a mangthangte;
Aw, khelhna meipi jing nuai a omte,
Hinna vak thu hilhlou ding i hi hiam;
Gam chih kil chih a om mite'n,
Tangtawn tangtawn hinna a theihna'ng un.

385 Ka Nu' Thumna

Ken mangngilh thei ngeikei hial ing,
Ka nu' thugen ken ka jak ni;
"Hon nusia ding maw, Bawi, tuin,
Na nu' thumna ngilh ngei ken," chi.

    Ka kiang' om bang Amah ka thei;
    Huihkhua pan aw huihkhi'n hon len,
    Ka nu' thumna hon theisak thak.

Ken mangngilh thei ngeikei hial ing,
Hon lungdamsak tawntung a aw;
Gamlapi ah ka taiman hang',
Ka nu' thumna thei gige ing.

Hunte bei zong mangngilh thei ke'ng,
Hon itna thu ka za lailai;
A tutna ngei a tu lai a,
Ka nu itpen thum in ka mu.

Ken mangngilh thei ngeikei hial ing,
Hondampa'n kei hon sinsak hun;
Ka khelh mawhna a thaisiat lai'
Tua ah ka nu' thumna dawng hi

    Eite vantung ah kimu ding;
    Tua van innpi ah tengkhawm ding,
    Ka nu' thumna dawnna hi ding.

    Toupa non panpih leh nangkia gingding,

387 Mikhial Ka Hi

388 Muang Om Nawn Ken

Lalhmingthang/Kamdinglien

Hunte tuibang in a liam a,
I khawvel damlai nite zong;
Ngak neilou in sun nichin in mual ah liam jel,
Khawvel pahna albang mangjel;
Zong in, nichin in ah nuam tang,
Muang om nawn ken, vualngaihte aw;
Tawpna ni a naita.

Hiai khawvel ah nopna zong in,
Sang tampi sihna in pi mang;
Hizong nopna mu leh neite nuamden omlou;
Muanna, bitna a chihlai un,
A tawpna un a honlap ding;
Muang om nawn ken, vualngaihte aw,
Tawpna'n honlap kha ding.

Aw, hongpai un vualngaihte aw,
Hotdamna thu hong ngaikhia un,
I Toupan hehpihna aw in a honsam hi;
Na hun kikhelsak sak nawn ken,
Na tawpna ding mulkimhuai hi;
Muang om nawn ken, vualngaihte aw,
Hun in ngak a neilou.

Sihna in zawhlah a neilou,
Natna in zong lauh a neilou,
Gawtmun in zong kuamah valhzawh louh a neilou;
Hotdamna thu na ngaih ken zaw,
Na tan ding zaw ka ngaingam lou;
Muang om nawn ken, vualngaihte aw,
Sihna in hon ngak hi.

@ Labu 2019

389 Ka Nunna'n Toupa Ngai

G.Hwl

Khuakhal tuiva luileng,
Gammang bang ka tau a;
Tujing singdawn a simbu hambang,
Khuakhal tui omlouhna,
Sakhi bang ka tau a;
Ka nunna'n Toupa ngaiin ka tauden e.

    Nang tawh lou in
    Nunna ching lou;
    Itna leh ngaihna Nang kiang a omte;
    Hong neisak kik aw, Toupa.

Mawhna guam sung a kia,
Sakhi thang awk bang in;
Mualsang khuva bang in ka tau a,
Ka omna khimkhua jing
Sung gilkial a na a;
Ka nunna'n Toupa ngaiin ka tauden e.

Vasa bang i kholh lai;
Nunnuam sian vontawi lia leh tang tawh,
Itna ningtui ka dawn
Lai nite ka ngai a;
Ka nunna'n Toupa ngai in ka tauden e.

391 Kikhopna Thupi!

Ira D. Sankey

Jing nisuak vak thupi bang a,
Pathian' Tapa hong kum chiang',
A vanglian vak khua vannuai a mi'n mu ding;
Kawl kimvel a namchih lai a
Ama' midik samkhawm ding;
Tatsa mite kikhopna thupi hi ding.

    Tungnungpen a kikhopna nuam,
    Nop kiamtheilou gam a kikhopna,
    Hehpihna gam tungnungpen' kikhopna,
    Tatsate tenna khawpi nuam
    Tungnungpen a kikhopna!

Thianmang tung a lungdamna mu,
Phamsa thelbang hong thawh chiang',
Hankhuk sung leh tuipi jalna tuangnungsia'n,
Kituakkhawm ding thangvan jawl ah
Tung kawlva bang lamtou ding;
Si leh hingte kituahkhawmna om ding hi.

Thangvan khawpi sunni bang tang,
Nat leh sat omlouhna gam;
Awlna luipi gei a i kimuh chiang in,
Thianmang siang ah phamsate tawh
Thangvan' nunnuam in leng ni,
Khen nawn lou dia kikhopna ni hi ding hi.

Toupa Jesu hong kum hun ding,
Niteng in hong nai deuhdeuh;
Mitphiat kal lou a limdanna ding hong nai;
A chiam ni thupi hong naita,
Mitphiat kal lou' limdang in,
Thangvan khawpi i tungtou ding, denchiang in.

410 Ni Thupi Pen Hongtung Ding

Lei gimhuai gam sihna mun a,
Tangtawn taikhuaval ngakte;
Lailung muanga na lusute,
Toupa tuak din phawng halh un.

    Ni thupipen tuang hongtung ding,
    Kawlni suak bang in i Toupa a hongvak dia;
    A aw ziak in han a omte thou ding,
    Van leh meipi kal ah;
    Khensate toh i Toupa
    Tuak din i lengtouta ding.

Lungkham kapte taiin nuam un,
Hun sawt lua ngak nawnlou ding;
Lungkham mauna in van a thawn,
Toupa ngaihdan buai nawn lou.

I Toupa' simthu chiam bangin,
Hun kilamdang thil hong thak;
Lungsim khial gilou silsiang in,
Laukha Siangthou samlut in.

Lei leh van thil tengteng sangin,
Munuam veng ka Hondampa,
Kei dia saron pak bang na lut-
Ni ding tuang hongtung sak in.

@ Labu 2019
